Base directory for this skill: C:\Users\ai\.claude\skills\memorytree-workflow

# MemoryTree

Use this skill for repo-level project memory. Do not treat it as an application runtime feature unless the user explicitly asks to productize it.

## On Activation

When this skill is invoked, immediately perform these steps without waiting for further user input:

1. Detect the repo state (not-installed, partial, or installed) using references/project-detection.md.
2. If not-installed: run scripts/init-memorytree.py to scaffold the workspace, then report what was created.
3. If partial: run scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py to add missing pieces, then report what was added.
4. If installed: read the active goal, bound todo, and latest chat log. Report the current state (goal summary, todo progress, pending tasks) and ask the user what they want to work on next.

Do not stop after detection to ask whether you should proceed. Act on the result immediately.

## Core Behavior

1. Detect the repo state before changing files. Use references/project-detection.md.
2. If MemoryTree is missing, initialize it with scripts/init-memorytree.py. If the script cannot run, create the files from assets/templates/.
3. If MemoryTree is partial, upgrade it with scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py before manual maintenance.
4. If MemoryTree is already installed, maintain only the active goal, bound todo, and current chat log. Use references/update-rules.md.
5. Keep the installation compatible with the host repo's branch, PR, CI, and review rules. Use references/git-policy.md.
6. Prefer safe defaults: do not add reply suffix requirements unless the host repository already requires them, do not mix code-and-memory commits by default, and do not override branch policy. MemoryTree-only git automation is allowed only inside the isolated flow in references/git-policy.md.
7. When locale is not explicit, choose it from repo language first, then system language. Use references/locale-selection.md.
8. Keep reply language aligned with user language first, then repo locale. Use references/response-language.md.
9. For partial repos, use the non-destructive upgrade path before manual maintenance. Use references/upgrade-path.md.
10. When transcript archival is enabled, import transcripts with deterministic code, preserve raw transcripts as evidence in both the current repo mirror and the global archive, generate cleaned Markdown for indexing, keep cross-project backfills and ambiguous ownership cases in the global archive only, and ask once per repository whether raw transcript files may be committed or pushed. Use references/transcript-archive.md.
11. When scripts are needed, prefer an existing uv run python environment first, then a system python, and only fall back to manual scaffolding or conservative manual review if no runner is available. Use references/execution-environment.md.

## Read Order

1. Repo AGENTS.md, if present.
2. Latest file in Memory/01_goals/.
3. Latest todo bound to that goal in Memory/02_todos/.
4. Memory/04_knowledge/ only when needed.
5. Memory/06_transcripts/clean/, transcript manifests, and repo-local raw transcript mirrors only when transcript history or cross-project memory search is relevant.
6. Memory/03_chat_logs/ and Memory/05_archive/ only when needed.

## Detect

1. Check whether Memory/ exists and matches the layout in references/memory-layout.md.
2. Classify the repo as not-installed, partial, or installed.
3. If the repo already has stronger rules than the generated templates, preserve the repo rules and only add missing MemoryTree pieces.

## Upgrade

1. Use scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py for repositories that already have AGENTS.md, custom policy files, or partial Memory/ content.
2. Preserve existing repo policy files by default.
3. Create only the missing MemoryTree pieces.
4. Read the upgrade result and treat agents_merge_required=true as a manual review task, not an overwrite instruction.
5. If no Python runner is available, do not create a project-local environment automatically. Fall back to conservative manual inspection and only make low-risk changes unless the user explicitly approved environment setup.

## Initialize

1. Run scripts/init-memorytree.py --root <repo> and pass --project-name, --goal-summary, and --locale when the user already provided them.
2. Use fresh init only when the repo does not already have AGENTS.md or another repo policy source such as a policy-bearing CONTRIBUTING.md, PR templates, CODEOWNERS, or commitlint config. If repo policy already exists, switch to scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py instead of trying to skip AGENTS.md.
3. Review the generated AGENTS.md before keeping it. Merge it with the repo's existing policy if needed.
4. Keep the initial installation minimal: Memory/01_goals, 02_todos, 03_chat_logs, optional 04_knowledge, 05_archive, and 06_transcripts only when transcript archival is enabled for the repo or needed for transcript import.
5. Use the locale-specific template files in assets/templates/<locale>/ as the source of truth for first-run scaffolding.
6. Prefer --locale auto when the user did not request a language explicitly.
7. Use scripts/detect-memorytree-locale.py when you need a deterministic locale check without scaffolding files.
8. Prefer uv run python first, then a system python. If neither is available, create first-run files directly from assets/templates/ instead of creating a project-local virtual environment by default.
9. If transcript archival is enabled for the repo, use scripts/import-transcripts.py for one explicit source file and scripts/discover-transcripts.py when scanning local client stores. Matching transcripts must update both the repo mirror and the global archive, while unrelated projects, ambiguous ownership cases, or mismatched explicit sources are archived in the global archive only. Let the scripts generate cleaned transcripts deterministically without spending model tokens on the cleaning step.
10. Ask once whether raw transcript files may also be committed to the repository. Record the answer in AGENTS.md, keep the files in the repo either way, and exclude raw files from automatic staging until the user says yes.

## Maintain

1. Change the active goal only after explicit user confirmation of a scope or requirement change.
2. Update the active todo when progress changes, milestones move, or the next task becomes clearer.
3. Append chat logs only. Never rewrite or delete prior entries.
4. Keep active files small. Move stale context to archive or knowledge files instead of bloating the active goal or todo.
5. Treat product ideas, architecture decisions, and operating constraints as goal or knowledge content. Treat step-by-step execution state as todo content.
6. Treat cleaned transcript indexes as discovery aids, not as the final source of truth. When exact wording matters, confirm against the raw transcript archive.
7. Prefer deterministic script-based transcript cleaning over manual rewriting. Do not spend model tokens to restate or normalize transcript content when scripts/import-transcripts.py can do it.
8. Reply in the user's language when clear; otherwise align with repo locale without rewriting existing files just to translate them.

## Git And Safety

1. Never assume MemoryTree can override the repo's branch model.
2. Default to isolated MemoryTree-only Git operations: stage only MemoryTree-owned files, use a MemoryTree-scoped commit title, push to a dedicated branch, and open a dedicated PR.
3. Enable auto-merge only for MemoryTree-only PRs, and only when the repository still enforces its required review and CI checks.
4. Keep repo-local raw transcript mirrors and the global transcript archive synchronized on every import. The global index must remain safe for concurrent multi-project updates.
5. Keep the repository mirror limited to transcripts that belong to the current repository. Unrelated or ambiguous transcripts belong in the global archive only.
6. Keep raw transcript files under Memory/06_transcripts/raw/** in the repo, but exclude them from automatic staging until the user explicitly approved raw transcript uploads for that repository.
7. If the diff mixes product code, shared policy files, cross-project transcript archives, or unclear ownership, stop and ask the user before committing or pushing.
8. If the repo has protected branches or PR-only rules, follow them even if older MemoryTree rules say otherwise.

## Resources

- references/project-detection.md: detect install state and choose init vs maintain.
- references/memory-layout.md: folder and file naming rules.
- references/update-rules.md: when to version goals, todos, and session logs.
- references/git-policy.md: safe Git defaults and policy merge guidance.
- references/locale-selection.md: locale choice rules and alias behavior.
- references/response-language.md: reply-language precedence and translation safety.
- references/transcript-archive.md: raw transcript archival, clean transcript indexing, per-client source rules, and repo upload confirmation rules.
- references/upgrade-path.md: safe adoption flow for partial repos.
- references/execution-environment.md: how to run MemoryTree scripts without assuming a project-local Python environment.
- assets/templates/en/ and assets/templates/zh-cn/: seed files for English and Simplified Chinese initialization.
- scripts/detect-memorytree-locale.py: print the effective locale for a target repository.
- scripts/discover-transcripts.py: scan supported local client stores, mirror current-project transcripts into the repo, and backfill other projects into the global archive only.
- scripts/import-transcripts.py: import one transcript into the repo mirror and global archive, then generate clean Markdown deterministically by code.
- scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py: safely add missing MemoryTree pieces to a partial repository.
- scripts/init-memorytree.py: deterministic scaffold script.

   203→   203→## Summary
   204→   204→
   205→   205→This repository appears to work as a Codex skill, but the current installation documentation is Claude Code-specific and can mislead Codex users into installing it into the wrong directory.
   206→   206→
   207→   207→The README says MemoryTree supports "Claude Code, Codex, Gemini CLI", but the install section only documents `~/.claude/skills/...`. In a Codex environment, that path is not where Codex discovers installed skills.
   208→   208→
   209→   209→There is also a second source of confusion: this repo itself is the skill (the `SKILL.md` file is at the repository root), so GitHub-based skill installers need to install the repo root as the skill path. That is not currently documented.
   210→   210→
   211→   211→## Evidence
   212→   212→
   213→   213→- The README explicitly says the project supports Codex.
   214→   214→- The install section only shows:

   218→   218→- `SKILL.md` is located at the repository root, which means the repo root is the skill directory

   228→   228→

   729→   729→
   730→   730→### 79. assistant
   731→   731→- Timestamp: `2026-03-16T04:29:22Z`
   732→   732→
   733→   733→不是 bug，属于它的设计。
   734→   734→
   735→   735→`~/.memorytree` 是这个 skill 的“用户级全局目录”，不是某个单独助手专用的目录。Claude Code、Codex、Gemini CLI 理论上都共享这一份全局数据。所以你之前在 Claude Code 里装过/用过 MemoryTree，导致现在 `C:\Users\ai\.memorytree\transcripts` 和索引库已经存在，这很正常。
   736→   736→
   737→   737→对 Codex 的影响是这样的：
   738→   738→
   739→   739→- 不会影响 `init`、`upgrade`、`daemon install` 这些基础操作。
   740→   740→- 也不会让当前 `openmnemo` 仓库出错。
   741→   741→- 会影响 `discover`、`recall`、跨项目搜索这类“读全局历史”的功能。
   742→   742→  影响方式不是冲突，而是它会把以前 Claude Code 的历史也当成可检索历史，这是它刻意支持的 cross-client 行为。
   743→   743→- 目前没有后台心跳在跑。
   744→   744→  我确认过 `Registered: no`，所以现在只是“全局历史数据存在”，不是“后台还在自动处理”。
   745→   745→
   746→   746→还有一个关键点：这台机器上只支持一个 MemoryTree 心跳任务，不分 Claude 还是 Codex。装上以后，它会作为同一个全局 heartbeat 工作，但真正处理哪些仓库，取决于 `~/.memorytree/config.toml` 里的 `projects` 列表。
   747→   747→
   748→   748→另外，`daemon install` 只会创建调度器和基础配置；如果不把 `D:\demo1\openmnemo` 注册进 `projects`，心跳其实什么都不会做。所以我建议这次这样配：
   749→   749→
   750→   750→- 间隔：`5m`
   751→   751→- `auto_push`：`false`
   752→   752→- scope：只注册当前仓库 `D:\demo1\openmnemo`
   753→   753→
   754→   754→如果你同意，我就按这组配置直接给你启用。
   755→   755→
   756→   756→### 80. user
   757→   757→- Timestamp: `2026-03-16T04:31:32Z`
   758→   758→
   759→   759→间隔5分钟   需要自动上传。  但是不理解你说的 scope 只注册当前仓库是什么意思  scope是什么意思呢   别的仓库怎办呢
   760→   760→
   761→   761→### 81. assistant
   762→   762→- Timestamp: `2026-03-16T04:31:56Z`
   763→   763→
   764→   764→`scope` 在这个 skill 里，意思是“心跳要负责哪些仓库”。
   765→   765→
   766→   766→不是指客户端范围，也不是指 Claude / Codex。它指的是 `~/.memorytree/config.toml` 里的 `projects` 列表。心跳每 5 分钟跑一次时，只会处理这个列表里的仓库。
   767→   767→
   768→   768→具体来说：
   769→   769→
   770→   770→- “只注册当前仓库”
   771→   771→  意思是只把 `D:\demo1\openmnemo` 写进 `config.toml` 的 `projects`。
   772→   772→  这样心跳只会管这个仓库的 transcript 导入、清理、提交、推送。
   773→   773→
   774→   774→- “别的仓库怎么办”
   775→   775→  别的仓库不会受影响，也不会自动处理。
   776→   776→  以后你想让某个仓库也接入，再把它加进 `projects` 就行。
   777→   777→
   778→   778→- “如果注册多个仓库”
   779→   779→  那一个全局 heartbeat 会统一处理这些仓库。
   780→   780→  这是它的设计：一台机器只有一个 heartbeat 任务，但它可以服务多个仓库。
   781→   781→
   782→   782→有个你必须知道的点：
   783→   783→
   784→   784→- `auto_push` 在这个实现里是全局配置，不是单仓库配置。
   785→   785→- 也就是说，如果你以后把 3 个仓库都注册进去，而且 `auto_push = true`，那这 3 个仓库都会自动推送。
   786→   786→
   787→   787→所以从安全角度，我建议先这样：
   788→   788→
   789→   789→- 间隔：`5m`
   790→   790→- `auto_push`: `true`
   791→   791→- scope：先只注册当前仓库 `D:\demo1\openmnemo`
   792→   792→
   793→   793→这样最稳。别的仓库以后需要时再逐个加，不会误推。
   794→   794→
   795→   795→如果你同意，我下一步就直接按这个 scope 给你启用。
   796→   796→

1→# MemoryTree 统一记忆仓库方案说明
     2→
     3→## 背景
     4→
     5→当前讨论的目标不是单纯给某一个项目加一个 `Memory/` 目录，而是要逐步形成一套长期可用的个人记忆资产系统。这个系统需要同时满足几件事：
     6→
     7→1. 所有聊天记录和记忆内容都能长期保存。
     8→2. 这些数据可以通过 GitHub 做同步和备份。
     9→3. 后续可以做统一检索和统一向量化。
    10→4. 每个项目又能保留只属于自己的记忆视图。
    11→
    12→用户已明确修正一个点：
    13→
    14→- 不按模型分层。
    15→- 只按工具分层，例如 `codex`、`claude`、`gemini`。
    16→
    17→
    18→## 核心判断
    19→
    20→### 我认同的部分
    21→
    22→以下方向是合理的：
    23→
    24→1. 个人记忆资产需要统一保管。
    25→2. 所有聊天内容都应该有完整总备份。
    26→3. 后续统一索引和统一向量化是重要方向。
    27→4. 目录结构需要按项目、按工具、按 `raw/clean/manifests` 分层。
    28→
    29→### 我不认同的部分
    30→
    31→我不建议把“全量所有项目记忆”复制到“每一个项目仓库的 `memorytree/*` 分支”里。
    32→
    33→原因：
    34→
    35→1. 同一份内容会在多个项目仓库里重复出现。
    36→2. 重复语料会让向量索引质量下降，召回结果容易被重复内容淹没。
    37→3. 某一个项目仓库权限变化时，其他项目记忆也会被连带暴露。
    38→4. 后续如果要删除、修正、脱敏，需要同时改很多份副本，维护成本很高。
    39→
    40→所以，“统一索引”不等于“复制到每个项目仓库”。
    41→
    42→
    43→## 推荐方案
    44→
    45→我建议使用两层存储结构，而不是每个项目都保存全量副本。
    46→
    47→### 第一层：总记忆仓库
    48→
    49→建立一个专门的私有仓库，例如：
    50→
    51→```text
    52→memorytree-vault
    53→```
    54→
    55→这个仓库是个人记忆资产的权威总库，保存所有项目的完整内容。
    56→
    57→### 第二层：项目镜像分支
    58→
    59→每个业务仓库内部仍然可以有自己的 `memorytree/*` 分支，例如：
    60→
    61→```text
    62→openmnemo
    63→  branch: memorytree/openmnemo
    64→```
    65→
    66→但这个项目分支只保存：
    67→
    68→- 属于 `openmnemo` 这个项目的记忆内容
    69→- 不保存其他项目的全量记忆
    70→
    71→
    72→## 通俗类比
    73→
    74→可以把它理解成三样东西：
    75→
    76→1. 业务仓库
    77→   - 比如 `openmnemo`
    78→   - 这是项目施工现场
    79→
    80→2. 项目镜像分支
    81→   - 比如 `memorytree/openmnemo`
    82→   - 这是这个项目自己的档案柜
    83→
    84→3. 总记忆仓库
    85→   - 比如 `memorytree-vault`
    86→   - 这是你的总档案馆
    87→
    88→项目档案柜可以有，但总档案馆不应该复制到每一个项目档案柜里。
    89→
    90→
    91→## 为什么这套方案更适合统一索引
    92→
    93→统一索引真正需要的是：
    94→
    95→1. 一个唯一的权威数据源。
    96→2. 一套统一元数据。
    97→3. 一套统一的索引过程。
    98→
    99→这三个条件都更适合放在总记忆仓库里完成。
   100→
   101→如果把同一份记忆复制到多个项目仓库里，再去做统一索引，会遇到：
   102→
   103→1. 大量重复数据。
   104→2. 去重逻辑变复杂。
   105→3. 项目边界不清楚。
   106→4. 索引和权限管理混在一起。
   107→
   108→因此：
   109→
   110→- 统一向量索引应该基于总记忆仓库。
   111→- 项目仓库的 `memorytree/*` 分支应该是项目镜像，而不是全量总库。
   112→
   113→
   114→## 目录结构建议
   115→
   116→### 总记忆仓库 `memorytree-vault`
   117→
   118→```text
   119→memorytree-vault/
   120→  projects/
   121→    openmnemo/
   122→      transcripts/
   123→        raw/
   124→          codex/2026/03/*.jsonl
   125→          claude/2026/03/*.jsonl
   126→          gemini/2026/03/*.jsonl
   127→        clean/
   128→          codex/2026/03/*.md
   129→          claude/2026/03/*.md
   130→          gemini/2026/03/*.md
   131→        manifests/
   132→          codex/2026/03/*.json
   133→          claude/2026/03/*.json
   134→          gemini/2026/03/*.json
   135→      memory/
   136→        goals/
   137→        todos/
   138→        chat-logs/
   139→    another-project/
   140→      ...
   141→  catalog/
   142→    sessions.jsonl
   143→```
   144→
   145→这里的层级是：
   146→
   147→1. 按项目分
   148→2. 项目内按内容类型分
   149→3. 内容类型下按工具分
   150→4. 再按年月分
   151→
   152→### 项目仓库中的镜像分支
   153→
   154→例如 `openmnemo` 仓库里的 `memorytree/openmnemo`：
   155→
   156→```text
   157→openmnemo
   158→  branch: memorytree/openmnemo
   159→    Memory/
   160→      01_goals/
   161→      02_todos/
   162→      03_chat_logs/
   163→      06_transcripts/
   164→        raw/
   165→          codex/
   166→          claude/
   167→          gemini/
   168→        clean/
   169→          codex/
   170→          claude/
   171→          gemini/
   172→        manifests/
   173→          codex/
   174→          claude/
   175→          gemini/
   176→```
   177→
   178→这个分支里只保留 `openmnemo` 本项目的内容。
   179→
   180→
   181→## 数据流建议
   182→
   183→推荐的数据流是：
   184→
   185→1. 用户在任意项目、任意代码分支中与 AI 对话。
   186→2. 新 transcript 先进入总记忆仓库对应的项目目录。
   187→3. 如果该 transcript 属于当前项目，再镜像到当前项目仓库的 `memorytree/*` 分支。
   188→4. 统一搜索和统一向量索引只从总记忆仓库构建。
   189→5. 项目内 PR、审查、同步则走本项目的 `memorytree/*` 分支。
   190→
   191→这样分工后：
   192→
   193→- 总记忆仓库负责“完整总账”
   194→- 项目镜像分支负责“项目视图”
   195→
   196→
   197→## 关于“一个项目是否要有两个记忆仓库”
   198→
   199→不是。
   200→
   201→更准确地说：
   202→
   203→1. 你个人只需要一个总记忆仓库 `memorytree-vault`
   204→2. 每个业务项目本来就有自己的业务仓库
   205→3. 业务仓库里可选有一个 `memorytree/*` 分支
   206→
   207→所以不是“每个项目建两个记忆仓库”，而是：
   208→
   209→- 一个全局共用的总记忆仓库
   210→- 多个业务项目各自保留自己的项目镜像分支
   211→
   212→
   213→## 最终结论
   214→
   215→公允判断如下：
   216→
   217→1. “个人记忆资产统一保管，并可同步到 GitHub”这个目标是合理的。
   218→2. “未来做统一向量索引”这个目标也是合理的。
   219→3. 但不应该把所有项目的全量记忆复制到每一个项目仓库的 `memorytree/*` 分支。
   220→4. 更合理的做法是：
   221→   - 用一个专门的总记忆仓库保存全量内容
   222→   - 用各项目自己的 `memorytree/*` 分支保存各自镜像
   223→   - 统一索引从总记忆仓库构建
   224→
   225→一句话概括：
   226→
   227→```text
   228→总记忆仓库负责全量数字资产，项目 memorytree 分支负责项目镜像，不负责承载所有项目的全量总账。
   229→```
   230→

1→# 记忆分类与聊天清洗规则
     2→
     3→## 目的
     4→
     5→这份文档用于定义一套适合长期使用的个人记忆资产分类法，以及 transcript 清洗逻辑。
     6→
     7→目标不是只服务一个短期项目，而是为未来几十年的个人数字资产管理做基础设计。
     8→
     9→本轮结论有两个前提：
    10→
    11→1. transcript 按工具分层，不按模型分层。
    12→2. 目录负责粗分类，索引负责精检索。
    13→
    14→
    15→## 一、分类总原则
    16→
    17→不要试图把所有维度都塞进目录层级里。
    18→
    19→目录应该只承载最稳定、最不容易变的维度：
    20→
    21→1. 这个记忆属于哪个范围
    22→2. 这个记忆属于哪个项目
    23→3. 这个记忆是什么类型
    24→4. 这个记忆来自哪个工具
    25→5. 这个记忆发生在什么时间段
    26→
    27→而这些变化快、组合多、后续可能扩展的维度，更适合放在元数据和索引里：
    28→
    29→1. branch
    30→2. tags
    31→3. topic
    32→4. people
    33→5. importance
    34→6. sensitivity
    35→7. workflow phase
    36→
    37→
    38→## 二、建议的分类维度
    39→
    40→建议整个系统统一使用以下维度。
    41→
    42→### 1. scope
    43→
    44→表示记忆归属范围。
    45→
    46→- `global`
    47→- `project`
    48→- `cross-project`
    49→- 后续可扩展 `personal`
    50→
    51→### 2. asset_type
    52→
    53→表示记忆类型。
    54→
    55→- `transcript`
    56→- `goal`
    57→- `todo`
    58→- `chat-log`
    59→- `knowledge`
    60→- `decision`
    61→- `archive`
    62→- `summary`
    63→
    64→### 3. source
    65→
    66→表示来源工具。
    67→
    68→- `codex`
    69→- `claude`
    70→- `gemini`
    71→
    72→### 4. derivation
    73→
    74→表示这是原始材料、清洗结果还是索引材料。
    75→
    76→- `raw`
    77→- `clean`
    78→- `manifest`
    79→- `summary`
    80→- `index`
    81→
    82→### 5. time
    83→
    84→时间维度建议按长期资产思路设计，而不是只按单次会话。
    85→
    86→- `decade`
    87→- `year`
    88→- `month`
    89→
    90→
    91→## 三、总记忆的分类方式
    92→
    93→总记忆是个人数字资产的总账。
    94→
    95→总记忆目录建议按下面这个顺序分类：
    96→
    97→1. 先按项目
    98→2. 再按记忆类型
    99→3. transcript 再按 `raw/clean/manifests`
   100→4. transcript 再按工具
   101→5. 最后按时间
   102→
   103→推荐结构：
   104→
   105→```text
   106→memorytree-vault/
   107→  projects/
   108→    openmnemo/
   109→      transcripts/
   110→        raw/
   111→          codex/2020s/2026/03/
   112→          claude/2020s/2026/03/
   113→          gemini/2020s/2026/03/
   114→        clean/
   115→          codex/2020s/2026/03/
   116→          claude/2020s/2026/03/
   117→          gemini/2020s/2026/03/
   118→        manifests/
   119→          codex/2020s/2026/03/
   120→          claude/2020s/2026/03/
   121→          gemini/2020s/2026/03/
   122→      memory/
   123→        active/
   124→          goals/
   125→          todos/
   126→          chat-logs/
   127→          knowledge/
   128→          decisions/
   129→        archive/
   130→          2020s/
   131→            2026/
   132→      summaries/
   133→        yearly/
   134→          2026.md
   135→        decade/
   136→          2020s.md
   137→    another-project/
   138→      ...
   139→  cross-project/
   140→  catalog/
   141→    sessions.jsonl
   142→```
   143→
   144→
   145→## 四、项目记忆的分类方式
   146→
   147→项目记忆不是总账，而是项目视图。
   148→
   149→因此项目内的分类不应该过细，重点应该是把“活跃内容”和“历史内容”分开。
   150→
   151→建议项目视图里至少有两层：
   152→
   153→1. `active`
   154→2. `archive`
   155→
   156→推荐结构：
   157→
   158→```text
   159→Memory/
   160→  01_active/
   161→    goals/
   162→    todos/
   163→    chat-logs/
   164→    knowledge/
   165→    decisions/
   166→  02_archive/
   167→    2020s/
   168→      2026/
   169→      2027/
   170→  03_transcripts/
   171→    raw/
   172→      codex/2020s/2026/03/
   173→      claude/2020s/2026/03/
   174→      gemini/2020s/2026/03/
   175→    clean/
   176→      codex/2020s/2026/03/
   177→      claude/2020s/2026/03/
   178→      gemini/2020s/2026/03/
   179→    manifests/
   180→      codex/2020s/2026/03/
   181→      claude/2020s/2026/03/
   182→      gemini/2020s/2026/03/
   183→  04_summaries/
   184→    yearly/
   185→      2026.md
   186→    decade/
   187→      2020s.md
   188→```
   189→
   190→如果为了兼容当前 skill 的目录，不想立刻调整成 `01_active/02_archive/03_transcripts`，也可以保留现有布局：
   191→
   192→- `01_goals`
   193→- `02_todos`
   194→- `03_chat_logs`
   195→- `04_knowledge`
   196→- `05_archive`
   197→- `06_transcripts`
   198→
   199→但建议把“十年 / 年 / 月”的概念逐步放进：
   200→
   201→- `05_archive`
   202→- `06_transcripts`
   203→- `summaries`
   204→
   205→
   206→## 五、时间维度怎么设计
   207→
   208→时间不能只靠文件名上的日期解决。
   209→
   210→对几十年的记忆资产来说，建议同时保留两种时间：
   211→
   212→### 1. event_time
   213→
   214→这是记忆真正发生的时间。
   215→
   216→例如：
   217→
   218→- transcript 的 `started_at`
   219→- goal 的创建或生效时间
   220→- decision 的确认时间
   221→
   222→目录主分类建议优先使用 `event_time`。
   223→
   224→### 2. ingest_time
   225→
   226→这是记忆进入系统的时间。
   227→
   228→它适合用于：
   229→
   230→- 审计
   231→- 回放
   232→- 排查
   233→
   234→但不适合作为主目录分类依据。
   235→
   236→### 3. 时间目录建议
   237→
   238→对于长期资产，建议使用：
   239→
   240→```text
   241→2020s/2026/03/
   242→```
   243→
   244→也就是：
   245→
   246→1. 十年
   247→2. 年
   248→3. 月
   249→
   250→这样几十年后结构仍然稳定，不会失控。
   251→
   252→
   253→## 六、哪些信息不应该做主目录
   254→
   255→以下信息很重要，但不建议作为主目录层级：
   256→
   257→### 1. branch
   258→
   259→原因：
   260→
   261→1. branch 变化太快
   262→2. 同一个项目可能有大量临时分支
   263→3. 如果目录按 branch 展开，很快会爆炸
   264→4. 同一条长期记忆不一定只属于一个 branch
   265→
   266→branch 更适合放在：
   267→
   268→- manifest
   269→- metadata
   270→- search index
   271→
   272→### 2. topic / tag
   273→
   274→topic 和 tag 更适合做索引字段，而不是目录字段。
   275→
   276→### 3. importance / sensitivity
   277→
   278→这些适合做策略标签，不适合变成目录树的一部分。
   279→
   280→
   281→## 七、聊天记录的清洗逻辑
   282→
   283→transcript 不应该只有一种形态，而应该分成三个层次。
   284→
   285→### 1. raw
   286→
   287→这是权威原件。
   288→
   289→特点：
   290→
   291→1. 保持原样
   292→2. 不做人为改写
   293→3. 用于审计和追溯
   294→4. 当 clean 有歧义时，以 raw 为准
   295→
   296→### 2. clean
   297→
   298→这是清洗后的可阅读文本。
   299→
   300→特点：
   301→
   302→1. 适合搜索
   303→2. 适合向量化
   304→3. 适合人工阅读
   305→4. 不是原始证据，只是整理后的表达
   306→
   307→### 3. manifest
   308→
   309→这是结构化元数据。
   310→
   311→manifest 应至少包含：
   312→
   313→1. `project`
   314→2. `client`
   315→3. `session_id`
   316→4. `started_at`
   317→5. `imported_at`
   318→6. `cwd`
   319→7. `branch`
   320→8. `raw_sha256`
   321→9. `raw_source_path`
   322→10. `message_count`
   323→11. `tool_event_count`
   324→12. `raw_upload_permission`
   325→
   326→
   327→## 八、clean transcript 应该怎么清洗
   328→
   329→clean 不是“总结”，而是“清理噪音后的可读 transcript”。
   330→
   331→### 应保留的内容
   332→
   333→1. 用户消息
   334→2. 助手消息
   335→3. 关键工具调用摘要
   336→4. 与任务推进相关的关键中间结论
   337→5. 时间、项目、工具、分支等核心元数据
   338→
   339→### 应弱化或折叠的内容
   340→
   341→1. 重复的元数据壳
   342→2. 低价值的队列事件
   343→3. 大量重复的工具调度噪音
   344→4. 超长、低信号的工具日志
   345→5. 对后续理解没有帮助的机械性输出
   346→
   347→### 不应做的事情
   348→
   349→1. 不要把 clean 改写成“模型总结”
   350→2. 不要为了好看而丢掉关键技术过程
   351→3. 不要让 clean 替代 raw
   352→4. 不要在 clean 里制造不存在的结论
   353→
   354→
   355→## 九、什么最适合做向量化
   356→
   357→向量化不应该直接把所有原始内容一股脑塞进去。
   358→
   359→建议分层：
   360→
   361→### 优先向量化
   362→
   363→1. `clean transcripts`
   364→2. `knowledge`
   365→3. `decisions`
   366→4. `yearly summaries`
   367→5. `decade summaries`
   368→
   369→### 次级向量化
   370→
   371→1. `chat-logs`
   372→2. `goals`
   373→3. `todos`
   374→
   375→### 不建议直接做主向量源
   376→
   377→1. `raw transcripts`
   378→2. 二进制缓存
   379→3. 纯噪音工具输出
   380→
   381→raw 更适合作为追溯证据，而不是主检索源。
   382→
   383→
   384→## 十、长期资产必须有汇总层
   385→
   386→如果系统只保存碎片，而没有年度和十年汇总，那它仍然很难成为真正的长期资产系统。
   387→
   388→因此建议强制保留两个汇总层：
   389→
   390→### 1. yearly summary
   391→
   392→每年一份。
   393→
   394→作用：
   395→
   396→1. 汇总这一年主要项目
   397→2. 汇总关键决策
   398→3. 汇总重要聊天主题
   399→4. 作为年级别入口
   400→
   401→### 2. decade summary
   402→
   403→每十年一份。
   404→
   405→作用：
   406→
   407→1. 压缩长期历史
   408→2. 形成真正的长期记忆骨架
   409→3. 避免几十年后只剩碎片
   410→
   411→
   412→## 十一、最终建议
   413→
   414→后续设计应坚持以下规则：
   415→
   416→1. 一切 transcript 都应同时有 `raw`、`clean`、`manifest` 三层。
   417→2. 目录只承载稳定维度：`project -> asset_type -> source -> time`。
   418→3. `branch`、`topic`、`tag` 等进入元数据和索引，不进入主目录。
   419→4. 时间按 `decade/year/month` 组织，而不是只靠文件名日期。
   420→5. 每个项目都应区分 `active` 和 `archive`。
   421→6. 每年和每十年都要生成汇总文档。
   422→
   423→一句话概括：
   424→
   425→```text

内容摘要：

memory-classification-and-cleaning_2026-03-16.md
定义了一套长期记忆资产的分类法和 transcript 清洗规则。核心结论：
- 目录只承载稳定维度（project → asset_type → source → time）
- branch/tag/topic 进元数据和索引，不进目录
- 时间按 decade/year/month 组织
- transcript 必须有 raw / clean / manifest 三层
- clean 是"清噪音后的可读版"，不是模型总结

memorytree-vault-architecture_2026-03-16.md
定义了两层存储架构：
- 第一层：memorytree-vault 总记忆仓库（全量权威总库，统一索引从这里构建）
- 第二层：各业务仓库的 memorytree/<project> 分支（只保存本项目镜像，不保存其他项目内容）

这两份文件是上次 session 里讨论出来的设计结论，已经沉淀到 knowledge 里了。你现在想基于这两份文档做什么？

    40→# MemoryTree
    41→
    42→Use this skill for repo-level project memory. Do not treat it as an application runtime feature unless the user explicitly asks to productize it.
    43→
    44→## On Activation
    45→
    46→When this skill is invoked, immediately perform these steps without waiting for further user input:
    47→
    48→1. Detect the repo state (`not-installed`, `partial`, or `installed`) using `references/project-detection.md`.
    49→2. If `not-installed`: run `scripts/init-memorytree.py` to scaffold the workspace, then report what was created.
    50→3. If `partial`: run `scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py` to add missing pieces, then report what was added.
    51→4. If `installed`: read the active goal, bound todo, and latest chat log. Report the current state (goal summary, todo progress, pending tasks) and ask the user what they want to work on next.
    52→
    53→Do not stop after detection to ask whether you should proceed. Act on the result immediately.
    54→
    55→## Core Behavior
    56→
    57→1. Detect the repo state before changing files. Use `references/project-detection.md`.
    58→2. If MemoryTree is missing, initialize it with `scripts/init-memorytree.py`. If the script cannot run, create the files from `assets/templates/`.
    59→3. If MemoryTree is partial, upgrade it with `scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py` before manual maintenance.
    60→4. If MemoryTree is already installed, maintain only the active goal, bound todo, and current chat log. Use `references/update-rules.md`.
    61→5. Keep the installation compatible with the host repo's branch, PR, CI, and review rules. Use `references/git-policy.md`.
    62→6. Prefer safe defaults: do not add reply suffix requirements unless the host repository already requires them, do not mix code-and-memory commits by default, and do not override branch policy. MemoryTree-only git automation is allowed only inside the isolated flow in `references/git-policy.md`.
    63→7. When locale is not explicit, choose it from repo language first, then system language. Use `references/locale-selection.md`.
    64→8. Keep reply language aligned with user language first, then repo locale. Use `references/response-language.md`.
    65→9. For partial repos, use the non-destructive upgrade path before manual maintenance. Use `references/upgrade-path.md`.
    66→10. When transcript archival is enabled, import transcripts with deterministic code, preserve raw transcripts as evidence in both the current repo mirror and the global archive, generate cleaned Markdown for indexing, keep cross-project backfills and ambiguous ownership cases in the global archive only, and ask once per repository whether raw transcript files may be committed or pushed. Use `references/transcript-archive.md`.
    67→11. When scripts are needed, prefer an existing `uv run python` environment first, then a system `python`, and only fall back to manual scaffolding or conservative manual review if no runner is available. Use `references/execution-environment.md`.
    68→
    69→## Read Order
    70→
    71→1. Repo `AGENTS.md`, if present.
    72→2. Latest file in `Memory/01_goals/`.
    73→3. Latest todo bound to that goal in `Memory/02_todos/`.
    74→4. `Memory/04_knowledge/` only when needed.
    75→5. `Memory/06_transcripts/clean/`, transcript manifests, and repo-local raw transcript mirrors only when transcript history or cross-project memory search is relevant.
    76→6. `Memory/03_chat_logs/` and `Memory/05_archive/` only when needed.
    77→
    78→## Detect
    79→
    80→1. Check whether `Memory/` exists and matches the layout in `references/memory-layout.md`.
    81→2. Classify the repo as `not-installed`, `partial`, or `installed`.
    82→3. If the repo already has stronger rules than the generated templates, preserve the repo rules and only add missing MemoryTree pieces.
    83→
    84→## Upgrade
    85→
    86→1. Use `scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py` for repositories that already have `AGENTS.md`, custom policy files, or partial `Memory/` content.
    87→2. Preserve existing repo policy files by default.
    88→3. Create only the missing MemoryTree pieces.
    89→4. Read the upgrade result and treat `agents_merge_required=true` as a manual review task, not an overwrite instruction.
    90→5. If no Python runner is available, do not create a project-local environment automatically. Fall back to conservative manual inspection and only make low-risk changes unless the user explicitly approved environment setup.
    91→
    92→## Initialize
    93→
    94→1. Run `scripts/init-memorytree.py --root <repo>` and pass `--project-name`, `--goal-summary`, and `--locale` when the user already provided them.
    95→2. Use fresh init only when the repo does not already have `AGENTS.md` or another repo policy source such as a policy-bearing `CONTRIBUTING.md`, PR templates, `CODEOWNERS`, or commitlint config. If repo policy already exists, switch to `scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py` instead of trying to skip `AGENTS.md`.
    96→3. Review the generated `AGENTS.md` before keeping it. Merge it with the repo's existing policy if needed.
    97→4. Keep the initial installation minimal: `Memory/01_goals`, `02_todos`, `03_chat_logs`, optional `04_knowledge`, `05_archive`, and `06_transcripts` only when transcript archival is enabled for the repo or needed for transcript import.
    98→5. Use the locale-specific template files in `assets/templates/<locale>/` as the source of truth for first-run scaffolding.
    99→6. Prefer `--locale auto` when the user did not request a language explicitly.
   100→7. Use `scripts/detect-memorytree-locale.py` when you need a deterministic locale check without scaffolding files.
   101→8. Prefer `uv run python` first, then a system `python`. If neither is available, create first-run files directly from `assets/templates/` instead of creating a project-local virtual environment by default.
   102→9. If transcript archival is enabled for the repo, use `scripts/import-transcripts.py` for one explicit source file and `scripts/discover-transcripts.py` when scanning local client stores. Matching transcripts must update both the repo mirror and the global archive, while unrelated projects, ambiguous ownership cases, or mismatched explicit sources are archived in the global archive only. Let the scripts generate cleaned transcripts deterministically without spending model tokens on the cleaning step.
   103→10. Ask once whether raw transcript files may also be committed to the repository. Record the answer in `AGENTS.md`, keep the files in the repo either way, and exclude `raw` files from automatic staging until the user says yes.
   104→
   105→## Maintain
   106→
   107→1. Change the active goal only after explicit user confirmation of a scope or requirement change.
   108→2. Update the active todo when progress changes, milestones move, or the next task becomes clearer.
   109→3. Append chat logs only. Never rewrite or delete prior entries.
   110→4. Keep active files small. Move stale context to archive or knowledge files instead of bloating the active goal or todo.
   111→5. Treat product ideas, architecture decisions, and operating constraints as goal or knowledge content. Treat step-by-step execution state as todo content.
   112→6. Treat cleaned transcript indexes as discovery aids, not as the final source of truth. When exact wording matters, confirm against the raw transcript archive.
   113→7. Prefer deterministic script-based transcript cleaning over manual rewriting. Do not spend model tokens to restate or normalize transcript content when `scripts/import-transcripts.py` can do it.
   114→8. Reply in the user's language when clear; otherwise align with repo locale without rewriting existing files just to translate them.
   115→
   116→## Git And Safety
   117→
   118→1. Never assume MemoryTree can override the repo's branch model.
   119→2. Default to isolated MemoryTree-only Git operations: stage only MemoryTree-owned files, use a MemoryTree-scoped commit title, push to a dedicated branch, and open a dedicated PR.
   120→3. Enable auto-merge only for MemoryTree-only PRs, and only when the repository still enforces its required review and CI checks.
   121→4. Keep repo-local raw transcript mirrors and the global transcript archive synchronized on every import. The global index must remain safe for concurrent multi-project updates.
   122→5. Keep the repository mirror limited to transcripts that belong to the current repository. Unrelated or ambiguous transcripts belong in the global archive only.
   123→6. Keep raw transcript files under `Memory/06_transcripts/raw/**` in the repo, but exclude them from automatic staging until the user explicitly approved raw transcript uploads for that repository.
   124→7. If the diff mixes product code, shared policy files, cross-project transcript archives, or unclear ownership, stop and ask the user before committing or pushing.
   125→8. If the repo has protected branches or PR-only rules, follow them even if older MemoryTree rules say otherwise.
   126→
   127→## Resources
   128→
   129→- `references/project-detection.md`: detect install state and choose init vs maintain.
   130→- `references/memory-layout.md`: folder and file naming rules.
   131→- `references/update-rules.md`: when to version goals, todos, and session logs.
   132→- `references/git-policy.md`: safe Git defaults and policy merge guidance.
   133→- `references/locale-selection.md`: locale choice rules and alias behavior.
   134→- `references/response-language.md`: reply-language precedence and translation safety.
   135→- `references/transcript-archive.md`: raw transcript archival, clean transcript indexing, per-client source rules, and repo upload confirmation rules.
   136→- `references/upgrade-path.md`: safe adoption flow for partial repos.
   137→- `references/execution-environment.md`: how to run MemoryTree scripts without assuming a project-local Python environment.
   138→- `assets/templates/en/` and `assets/templates/zh-cn/`: seed files for English and Simplified Chinese initialization.
   139→- `scripts/detect-memorytree-locale.py`: print the effective locale for a target repository.
   140→- `scripts/discover-transcripts.py`: scan supported local client stores, mirror current-project transcripts into the repo, and backfill other projects into the global archive only.
   141→- `scripts/import-transcripts.py`: import one transcript into the repo mirror and global archive, then generate clean Markdown deterministically by code.
   142→- `scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py`: safely add missing MemoryTree pieces to a partial repository.
   143→- `scripts/init-memorytree.py`: deterministic scaffold script.

找到了。raw 文件里完整保存了所有中文对话内容，包括你的提问和 Codex 的中文回答。

问题出在 clean transcript 的生成方式上——deterministic-code 模式把消息内容按结构提取，但 Codex 的 raw 格式里用户消息和助手消息都嵌在 payload.text 里，清洗脚本没有正确识别这个结构，导致 clean 版本里只有消息编号和时间戳，实际文字内容丢失了。

也就是说：
- raw 文件：完整，中文对话全在
- clean 文件：只有骨架，内容丢了

这是 memorytree-workflow 的 clean 脚本对 Codex 格式解析不完整的 bug。你要不要给上游再提一个 issue？

1→/**
     2→ * Transcript parsing — client inference, dispatch, and format-specific parsers.
     3→ * Port of scripts/_transcript_parse.py

     6→import { readFileSync, statSync } from 'node:fs'
     7→import { basename, extname } from 'node:path'
     8→
     9→import type { Client, ParsedTranscript, TranscriptMessage, TranscriptToolEvent } from '../types/transcript.js'
    10→import { toPosixPath } from '../utils/path.js'
    11→import {
    12→  SKIP_BLOCK_TYPES,
    13→  TEXT_BLOCK_TYPES,
    14→  TOOL_RESULT_TYPES,
    15→  TOOL_USE_TYPES,
    16→  deduplicateMessages,
    17→  deduplicateToolEvents,
    18→  earliestTimestamp,

    31→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    32→// Client inference + dispatch
    33→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    34→
    35→export function inferClient(client: string, sourcePath: string): Client {
    36→  if (client !== 'auto') {
    37→    return client as Client
    38→  }
    39→  const normalized = toPosixPath(sourcePath).toLowerCase()
    40→  const fileName = basename(sourcePath).toLowerCase()
    41→  if (normalized.includes('/.codex/') || fileName.startsWith('rollout-')) {
    42→    return 'codex'
    43→  }
    44→  if (normalized.includes('/.claude/') || normalized.includes('/projects/')) {
    45→    return 'claude'
    46→  }
    47→  if (normalized.includes('/.gemini/') || normalized.includes('checkpoint')) {
    48→    return 'gemini'
    49→  }
    50→  throw new Error(`could not infer transcript client from source path: ${sourcePath}`)
    51→}
    52→
    53→export function parseTranscript(client: string, sourcePath: string): ParsedTranscript {
    54→  const resolved = inferClient(client, sourcePath)
    55→  if (resolved === 'codex') {
    56→    return parseCodexTranscript(sourcePath)
    57→  }
    58→  if (resolved === 'claude') {
    59→    return parseClaudeTranscript(sourcePath)
    60→  }
    61→  if (resolved === 'gemini') {
    62→    return parseGeminiTranscript(sourcePath)
    63→  }
    64→  throw new Error(`unsupported transcript client: ${resolved}`)
    65→}
    66→
    67→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    68→// Codex parser
    69→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

    71→export function parseCodexTranscript(filePath: string): ParsedTranscript {
    72→  const records = loadJsonl(filePath)
    73→  const stem = basename(filePath, extname(filePath))
    74→  let sessionId = stem
    75→  let title = stem
    76→  let startedAt = normalizeTimestamp(statSync(filePath).mtimeMs / 1000)
    77→  let cwd = ''
    78→  let branch = ''
    79→  const messages: TranscriptMessage[] = []
    80→  const toolEvents: TranscriptToolEvent[] = []
    81→
    82→  for (const record of records) {
    83→    const recordType = String(record['type'] ?? '')
    84→    const timestamp = normalizeTimestamp(record['timestamp'], startedAt)
    85→
    86→    if (recordType === 'session_meta') {
    87→      const payload = ensureDict(record['payload'])
    88→      sessionId = String(payload['id'] ?? '') || sessionId
    89→      title = String(payload['thread_name'] ?? '') || String(payload['title'] ?? '') || title
    90→      startedAt = earliestTimestamp(startedAt, payload['timestamp'])
    91→      cwd = String(payload['cwd'] ?? '') || cwd
    92→      branch = String(getNested(payload, 'git', 'branch') ?? '') || branch
    93→      continue
    94→    }
    95→
    96→    if (recordType !== 'response_item' && recordType !== 'event_msg') {
    97→      continue
    98→    }
    99→
   100→    const payload = ensureDict(record['payload'])
   101→    const payloadType = String(payload['type'] ?? '')
   102→
   103→    if (payloadType === 'message') {
   104→      const role = String(payload['role'] ?? '').toLowerCase()
   105→      if (role === 'user' || role === 'assistant') {
   106→        const text = extractTextBlocks(payload['content'])
   107→        if (text) {
   108→          messages.push({ role, text, timestamp })
   109→        }
   110→      }
   111→      continue
   112→    }
   113→
   114→    if (payloadType === 'user_message' || payloadType === 'agent_message') {
   115→      const role = payloadType === 'user_message' ? 'user' : 'assistant'
   116→      const text = String(payload['message'] ?? '').trim()
   117→      if (text) {
   118→        messages.push({ role, text, timestamp })
   119→      }
   120→      continue
   121→    }
   122→
   123→    if (payloadType === 'function_call') {
   124→      const name = String(payload['name'] ?? '') || 'function_call'
   125→      const args = payload['arguments'] ?? payload['input']
   126→      toolEvents.push({
   127→        summary: `${name} input=${summarizeValue(args)}`,
   128→        timestamp,
   129→      })
   130→      continue
   131→    }
   132→
   133→    if (payloadType === 'custom_tool_call') {
   134→      const name = String(payload['name'] ?? '') || String(payload['call_id'] ?? '') || 'custom_tool_call'
   135→      toolEvents.push({
   136→        summary: `${name} input=${summarizeValue(payload['input'])}`,
   137→        timestamp,
   138→      })
   139→      continue
   140→    }
   141→
   142→    if (payloadType === 'function_call_output') {
   143→      const name = String(payload['name'] ?? '') || String(payload['call_id'] ?? '') || 'function_call_output'
   144→      const output = payload['output'] ?? payload['content']
   145→      toolEvents.push({
   146→        summary: `${name} output=${summarizeValue(output)}`,
   147→        timestamp,
   148→      })
   149→      continue
   150→    }
   151→
   152→    if (payloadType === 'custom_tool_call_output') {
   153→      const name = String(payload['name'] ?? '') || String(payload['call_id'] ?? '') || 'custom_tool_call_output'
   154→      const output = payload['output'] ?? payload['content']
   155→      toolEvents.push({
   156→        summary: `${name} output=${summarizeValue(output)}`,
   157→        timestamp,
   158→      })
   159→    }
   160→  }
   161→
   162→  return {
   163→    client: 'codex',
   164→    session_id: sessionId,
   165→    title,
   166→    started_at: startedAt,
   167→    cwd,
   168→    branch,
   169→    messages: deduplicateMessages(messages),
   170→    tool_events: deduplicateToolEvents(toolEvents),
   171→    source_path: filePath,
   172→  }
   173→}
   174→
   175→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   176→// Claude parser
   177→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   178→
   179→export function parseClaudeTranscript(filePath: string): ParsedTranscript {
   180→  const records = loadJsonl(filePath)
   181→  const stem = basename(filePath, extname(filePath))
   182→  let sessionId = stem
   183→  const title = stem
   184→  let startedAt = normalizeTimestamp(statSync(filePath).mtimeMs / 1000)
   185→  let cwd = ''
   186→  let branch = ''
   187→  const messages: TranscriptMessage[] = []
   188→  const toolEvents: TranscriptToolEvent[] = []
   189→
   190→  for (const record of records) {
   191→    const recordType = String(record['type'] ?? '')
   192→    const timestamp = normalizeTimestamp(record['timestamp'], startedAt)
   193→    sessionId = String(record['sessionId'] ?? '') || sessionId
   194→    startedAt = earliestTimestamp(startedAt, record['timestamp'])
   195→    cwd = String(record['cwd'] ?? '') || cwd
   196→    branch = String(record['gitBranch'] ?? '') || branch
   197→
   198→    if (recordType !== 'user' && recordType !== 'assistant') {
   199→      continue
   200→    }
   201→
   202→    const message = ensureDict(record['message'])
   203→    const role = String(message['role'] ?? '').toLowerCase() || recordType
   204→    const textParts: string[] = []
   205→    const content = message['content']
   206→
   207→    if (typeof content === 'string') {
   208→      const text = content.trim()
   209→      if ((role === 'user' || role === 'assistant') && text) {
   210→        messages.push({ role, text, timestamp })
   211→      }
   212→      continue
   213→    }
   214→
   215→    for (const block of ensureList(content)) {
   216→      if (typeof block === 'string') {
   217→        if (block.trim()) {
   218→          textParts.push(block.trim())
   219→        }
   220→        continue
   221→      }
   222→      if (block === null || typeof block !== 'object' || Array.isArray(block)) {
   223→        continue
   224→      }
   225→      const rec = block as Record<string, unknown>
   226→      const blockType = String(rec['type'] ?? '').toLowerCase()
   227→
   228→      if (TEXT_BLOCK_TYPES.has(blockType)) {
   229→        const text = String(rec['text'] ?? '').trim()
   230→        if (text) {
   231→          textParts.push(text)
   232→        }
   233→        continue
   234→      }
   235→      if (SKIP_BLOCK_TYPES.has(blockType)) {
   236→        continue
   237→      }
   238→      if (TOOL_USE_TYPES.has(blockType)) {
   239→        const name = String(rec['name'] ?? '') || 'tool_use'
   240→        toolEvents.push({
   241→          summary: `${name} input=${summarizeValue(rec['input'])}`,
   242→          timestamp,
   243→        })
   244→        continue
   245→      }
   246→      if (TOOL_RESULT_TYPES.has(blockType)) {
   247→        const toolUseId = String(rec['tool_use_id'] ?? '') || 'tool_result'
   248→        toolEvents.push({
   249→          summary: `${toolUseId} output=${summarizeValue(rec['content'])}`,
   250→          timestamp,
   251→        })
   252→      }
   253→    }
   254→
   255→    const text = joinParagraphs(textParts)
   256→    if ((role === 'user' || role === 'assistant') && text) {
   257→      messages.push({ role, text, timestamp })
   258→    }
   259→  }
   260→
   261→  return {
   262→    client: 'claude',
   263→    session_id: sessionId,
   264→    title,
   265→    started_at: startedAt,
   266→    cwd,
   267→    branch,
   268→    messages: deduplicateMessages(messages),
   269→    tool_events: deduplicateToolEvents(toolEvents),
   270→    source_path: filePath,
   271→  }
   272→}
   273→
   274→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   275→// Gemini parser
   276→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   277→
   278→export function parseGeminiTranscript(filePath: string): ParsedTranscript {
   279→  const stem = basename(filePath, extname(filePath))
   280→  let sessionId = stem
   281→  const title = stem
   282→  let startedAt = normalizeTimestamp(statSync(filePath).mtimeMs / 1000)
   283→  let cwd = ''
   284→  let branch = ''
   285→  const messages: TranscriptMessage[] = []
   286→  const toolEvents: TranscriptToolEvent[] = []
   287→
   288→  let payload: unknown
   289→  if (extname(filePath).toLowerCase() === '.jsonl') {
   290→    payload = loadJsonl(filePath)
   291→  } else {
   292→    payload = JSON.parse(readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8')) as unknown
   293→  }
   294→
   295→  const metaKeys: ReadonlySet<string> = new Set(['sessionId', 'chatId', 'cwd', 'branch', 'timestamp'])
   296→  const firstMeta = findFirstMappingWithKeys(payload, metaKeys)
   297→  if (firstMeta !== null) {
   298→    sessionId = String(firstMeta['sessionId'] ?? '') || String(firstMeta['chatId'] ?? '') || String(firstMeta['id'] ?? '') || sessionId
   299→    startedAt = earliestTimestamp(startedAt, firstMeta['timestamp'])
   300→    cwd = String(firstMeta['cwd'] ?? '') || String(firstMeta['projectRoot'] ?? '') || cwd
   301→    branch = String(firstMeta['branch'] ?? '') || branch
   302→  }
   303→
   304→  function visit(node: unknown): void {
   305→    if (Array.isArray(node)) {
   306→      for (const item of node) {
   307→        visit(item)
   308→      }
   309→      return
   310→    }
   311→    if (node === null || typeof node !== 'object') {
   312→      return
   313→    }
   314→    const rec = node as Record<string, unknown>
   315→
   316→    sessionId = String(rec['sessionId'] ?? '') || String(rec['chatId'] ?? '') || String(rec['id'] ?? '') || sessionId
   317→    startedAt = earliestTimestamp(startedAt, rec['timestamp'])
   318→    cwd = String(rec['cwd'] ?? '') || String(rec['projectRoot'] ?? '') || cwd
   319→    branch = String(rec['branch'] ?? '') || branch
   320→
   321→    const role = String(rec['role'] ?? rec['author'] ?? rec['sender'] ?? '').toLowerCase()
   322→    const timestamp = normalizeTimestamp(rec['timestamp'], startedAt)
   323→
   324→    if (role === 'user' || role === 'assistant' || role === 'model') {
   325→      const normalizedRole = role === 'model' ? 'assistant' : role
   326→      const text = extractGeminiText(rec)
   327→      if (text) {
   328→        messages.push({ role: normalizedRole, text, timestamp })
   329→      }
   330→    }
   331→
   332→    const toolName =
   333→      getNested(rec, 'toolUse', 'name') ??
   334→      rec['toolName'] ??
   335→      rec['functionName'] ??
   336→      rec['tool']
   337→    if (toolName) {
   338→      toolEvents.push({
   339→        summary: `${String(toolName)} input=${summarizeValue(rec['args'] ?? rec['input'])}`,
   340→        timestamp,
   341→      })
   342→    }
   343→
   344→    for (const value of Object.values(rec)) {
   345→      visit(value)
   346→    }
   347→  }
   348→
   349→  visit(payload)
   350→
   351→  return {
   352→    client: 'gemini',
   353→    session_id: sessionId,
   354→    title,
   355→    started_at: startedAt,
   356→    cwd,
   357→    branch,
   358→    messages: deduplicateMessages(messages),
   359→    tool_events: deduplicateToolEvents(toolEvents),
   360→    source_path: filePath,
   361→  }
   362→}

   178→export function preserveExistingImportTimestamp(
   179→  existing: Record<string, unknown> | null,
   180→  payload: ManifestEntry,
   181→): ManifestEntry {
   182→  if (existing === null) return payload

   185→  const importedAt = existing['imported_at']

   187→    return { ...payload, imported_at: importedAt }

   192→export function manifestSignature(payload: Record<string, unknown>): Record<string, unknown> {
   193→  const result: Record<string, unknown> = {}

   195→    if (key !== 'imported_at') {
   196→      result[key] = value
   197→    }

   229→function stemOf(filePath: string): string {
   230→  const base = basename(filePath)
   231→  const ext = extname(base)
   232→  return ext ? base.slice(0, -ext.length) : base

   235→function deepEqual(a: unknown, b: unknown): boolean {
   236→  if (a === b) return true
   237→  if (a === null || b === null || typeof a !== typeof b) return false
   238→  if (typeof a !== 'object') return false
   239→  if (Array.isArray(a) !== Array.isArray(b)) return false
   240→  const aObj = a as Record<string, unknown>
   241→  const bObj = b as Record<string, unknown>
   242→  const aKeys = Object.keys(aObj)
   243→  const bKeys = Object.keys(bObj)
   244→  if (aKeys.length !== bKeys.length) return false
   245→  return aKeys.every(key => deepEqual(aObj[key], bObj[key]))
   246→}

    29→export function slugify(value: string, fallback = 'session'): string {
    30→  // eslint-disable-next-line no-control-regex
    31→  const asciiValue = value.replace(/[^\x00-\x7F]/g, '').toLowerCase()
    32→  const slug = asciiValue.replace(/[^a-z0-9._-]+/g, '-').replace(/^[-._]+|[-._]+$/g, '')
    33→  return slug || fallback
    34→}

    36→export function sha256File(filePath: string): string {

    41→export function contentHash(text: string): string {

    45→export function normalizeTimestamp(value: unknown, fallback?: string | null): string {
    46→  if (typeof value === 'number') {
    47→    // Always treat as Unix seconds (matching Python's datetime.fromtimestamp)
    48→    const d = new Date(value * 1000)
    49→    return formatUtcIso(d)
    50→  }
    51→
    52→  if (value instanceof Date) {
    53→    return formatUtcIso(value)
    54→  }
    55→
    56→  if (typeof value === 'string') {
    57→    const text = value.trim()
    58→    if (!text) {
    59→      return fallback ?? normalizeTimestamp(new Date())
    60→    }
    61→    const parsed = parseIsoTimestamp(text)
    62→    if (parsed !== null) {
    63→      return formatUtcIso(parsed)
    64→    }
    65→    return text
    66→  }
    67→
    68→  return fallback ?? normalizeTimestamp(new Date())
    69→}
    70→
    71→export function earliestTimestamp(current: string, candidate: unknown): string {
    72→  const normalized = normalizeTimestamp(candidate, current)
    73→  const currentDt = parseIsoTimestamp(current)
    74→  const normalizedDt = parseIsoTimestamp(normalized)
    75→  if (currentDt !== null && normalizedDt !== null) {
    76→    return normalizedDt < currentDt ? normalized : current
    77→  }
    78→  if (normalizedDt !== null) {
    79→    return normalized
    80→  }
    81→  return current || normalized
    82→}
    83→
    84→export function parseIsoTimestamp(value: string): Date | null {
    85→  if (!value) return null
    86→  let candidate = value
    87→  if (candidate.endsWith('Z')) {
    88→    candidate = candidate.slice(0, -1) + '+00:00'
    89→  } else if (!/[+-]\d{2}:\d{2}$/.test(candidate) && !/[+-]\d{4}$/.test(candidate)) {
    90→    // No timezone offset — treat as UTC (matching Python behavior)
    91→    candidate = candidate + '+00:00'
    92→  }
    93→  const d = new Date(candidate)
    94→  if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return null
    95→  return d
    96→}

    98→export function timestampPartition(timestamp: string): [string, string] {
    99→  const d = parseIsoTimestamp(timestamp)
   100→  if (d === null) return ['unknown', 'unknown']
   101→  const year = d.getUTCFullYear().toString()
   102→  const month = (d.getUTCMonth() + 1).toString().padStart(2, '0')
   103→  return [year, month]
   104→}

   115→export function summarizeValue(value: unknown, limit = 180): string {
   116→  if (value === null || value === undefined) return 'none'

   123→    text = JSON.stringify(sortKeysDeep(value))
   124→  } catch {
   125→    text = String(value)
   126→  }
   127→  text = text.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim()
   128→  return truncate(text, limit)
   129→}

   155→export function getNested(payload: Record<string, unknown>, ...keys: string[]): unknown {
   156→  let current: unknown = payload
   157→  for (const key of keys) {
   158→    if (current === null || typeof current !== 'object' || Array.isArray(current)) {
   159→      return null
   160→    }
   161→    current = (current as Record<string, unknown>)[key]
   162→  }
   163→  return current ?? null
   164→}

   166→export function loadJsonl(filePath: string): Record<string, unknown>[] {
   167→  let content: string
   168→  try {
   169→    content = readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8')
   170→  } catch {
   171→    return []
   172→  }
   173→  const records: Record<string, unknown>[] = []
   174→  for (const line of content.split('\n')) {
   175→    const trimmed = line.trim()
   176→    if (!trimmed) continue
   177→    try {
   178→      records.push(JSON.parse(trimmed) as Record<string, unknown>)
   179→    } catch {
   180→      continue
   181→    }
   182→  }
   183→  return records
   184→}

   186→export function loadJson(filePath: string): Record<string, unknown> | null {
   187→  if (!existsSync(filePath)) return null
   188→  try {
   189→    const text = readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8')
   190→    return JSON.parse(text) as Record<string, unknown>
   191→  } catch {
   192→    return null
   193→  }
   194→}

   196→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   197→// Text extraction helpers
   198→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   199→
   200→export function extractTextBlocks(blocks: unknown): string {
   201→  const parts: string[] = []
   202→
   203→  for (const block of ensureList(blocks)) {
   204→    if (typeof block === 'string') {
   205→      const text = block.trim()
   206→      if (text) parts.push(text)
   207→      continue
   208→    }
   209→    if (block === null || typeof block !== 'object' || Array.isArray(block)) continue
   210→
   211→    const rec = block as Record<string, unknown>
   212→    const blockType = String(rec['type'] ?? '').toLowerCase()
   213→    if (ALL_SKIP_TYPES.has(blockType)) continue
   214→    if (TEXT_BLOCK_TYPES.has(blockType)) {
   215→      const text = String(rec['text'] ?? '').trim()
   216→      if (text) parts.push(text)
   217→      continue
   218→    }
   219→    const fallbackText = extractSimpleText(block)
   220→    if (fallbackText) parts.push(fallbackText)
   221→  }
   222→  return joinParagraphs(parts)
   223→}
   224→
   225→export function extractSimpleText(value: unknown): string {
   226→  if (typeof value === 'string') return value.trim()
   227→  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
   228→    return joinParagraphs(value.map(item => extractSimpleText(item)))
   229→  }
   230→  if (value !== null && typeof value === 'object') {
   231→    const rec = value as Record<string, unknown>
   232→    for (const key of ['text', 'content', 'value']) {
   233→      if (key in rec && typeof rec[key] === 'string') {
   234→        return (rec[key] as string).trim()
   235→      }
   236→    }
   237→    return ''
   238→  }
   239→  return ''
   240→}
   241→
   242→export function extractGeminiText(node: Record<string, unknown>): string {
   243→  const parts: string[] = []
   244→  for (const key of ['parts', 'content', 'text', 'message']) {
   245→    parts.push(...extractGeminiParts(node[key]))
   246→  }
   247→  return joinParagraphs(parts)
   248→}
   249→
   250→export function extractGeminiParts(value: unknown): string[] {
   251→  if (typeof value === 'string') {
   252→    const text = value.trim()
   253→    return text ? [text] : []
   254→  }
   255→  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
   256→    const parts: string[] = []
   257→    for (const item of value) {
   258→      parts.push(...extractGeminiParts(item))
   259→    }
   260→    return parts
   261→  }
   262→  if (value !== null && typeof value === 'object') {
   263→    const rec = value as Record<string, unknown>
   264→    const blockType = String(rec['type'] ?? '').toLowerCase()
   265→    if (ALL_SKIP_TYPES.has(blockType)) return []
   266→    if ('text' in rec && typeof rec['text'] === 'string') {
   267→      const text = (rec['text'] as string).trim()
   268→      return text ? [text] : []
   269→    }
   270→    const parts: string[] = []
   271→    for (const key of ['parts', 'content']) {
   272→      if (key in rec) {
   273→        parts.push(...extractGeminiParts(rec[key]))
   274→      }
   275→    }
   276→    return parts
   277→  }
   278→  return []
   279→}
   280→
   281→export function findFirstMappingWithKeys(value: unknown, keys: ReadonlySet<string>): Record<string, unknown> | null {
   282→  if (value !== null && typeof value === 'object' && !Array.isArray(value)) {
   283→    const rec = value as Record<string, unknown>
   284→    const recKeys = Object.keys(rec)
   285→    if (recKeys.some(k => keys.has(k))) return rec
   286→    for (const v of Object.values(rec)) {
   287→      const result = findFirstMappingWithKeys(v, keys)
   288→      if (result !== null) return result
   289→    }
   290→    return null
   291→  }
   292→  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
   293→    for (const item of value) {
   294→      const result = findFirstMappingWithKeys(item, keys)
   295→      if (result !== null) return result
   296→    }
   297→  }
   298→  return null
   299→}
   300→
   301→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   302→// Deduplication helpers
   303→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   304→
   305→export function deduplicateMessages(messages: readonly TranscriptMessage[]): TranscriptMessage[] {
   306→  const seen = new Set<string>()
   307→  const result: TranscriptMessage[] = []
   308→  for (const msg of messages) {
   309→    const sig = `${msg.timestamp ?? ''}\0${msg.role}\0${contentHash(msg.text)}`
   310→    if (!seen.has(sig)) {
   311→      seen.add(sig)
   312→      result.push(msg)
   313→    }
   314→  }
   315→  return result
   316→}
   317→
   318→export function deduplicateToolEvents(events: readonly TranscriptToolEvent[]): TranscriptToolEvent[] {
   319→  const seen = new Set<string>()
   320→  const result: TranscriptToolEvent[] = []
   321→  for (const evt of events) {
   322→    const sig = `${evt.timestamp ?? ''}\0${contentHash(evt.summary)}`
   323→    if (!seen.has(sig)) {
   324→      seen.add(sig)
   325→      result.push(evt)
   326→    }
   327→  }
   328→  return result
   329→}
   330→
   331→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   332→// Internal helpers
   333→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   334→
   335→function sortKeysDeep(value: unknown): unknown {
   336→  if (Array.isArray(value)) return value.map(sortKeysDeep)
   337→  if (value !== null && typeof value === 'object') {
   338→    const sorted: Record<string, unknown> = {}
   339→    for (const key of Object.keys(value as Record<string, unknown>).sort()) {
   340→      sorted[key] = sortKeysDeep((value as Record<string, unknown>)[key])
   341→    }
   342→    return sorted
   343→  }
   344→  return value
   345→}
   346→
   347→function formatUtcIso(d: Date): string {
   348→  const year = d.getUTCFullYear()
   349→  const month = String(d.getUTCMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')
   350→  const day = String(d.getUTCDate()).padStart(2, '0')
   351→  const hours = String(d.getUTCHours()).padStart(2, '0')
   352→  const minutes = String(d.getUTCMinutes()).padStart(2, '0')
   353→  const seconds = String(d.getUTCSeconds()).padStart(2, '0')
   354→  return `${year}-${month}-${day}T${hours}:${minutes}:${seconds}Z`
   355→}

71→export function parseCodexTranscript(filePath: string): ParsedTranscript {
    72→  const records = loadJsonl(filePath)
    73→  const stem = basename(filePath, extname(filePath))
    74→  let sessionId = stem
    75→  let title = stem
    76→  let startedAt = normalizeTimestamp(statSync(filePath).mtimeMs / 1000)
    77→  let cwd = ''
    78→  let branch = ''
    79→  const messages: TranscriptMessage[] = []
    80→  const toolEvents: TranscriptToolEvent[] = []
    81→
    82→  for (const record of records) {
    83→    const recordType = String(record['type'] ?? '')
    84→    const timestamp = normalizeTimestamp(record['timestamp'], startedAt)
    85→
    86→    if (recordType === 'session_meta') {
    87→      const payload = ensureDict(record['payload'])
    88→      sessionId = String(payload['id'] ?? '') || sessionId
    89→      title = String(payload['thread_name'] ?? '') || String(payload['title'] ?? '') || title
    90→      startedAt = earliestTimestamp(startedAt, payload['timestamp'])
    91→      cwd = String(payload['cwd'] ?? '') || cwd
    92→      branch = String(getNested(payload, 'git', 'branch') ?? '') || branch
    93→      continue
    94→    }
    95→
    96→    if (recordType !== 'response_item' && recordType !== 'event_msg') {
    97→      continue
    98→    }
    99→
   100→    const payload = ensureDict(record['payload'])
   101→    const payloadType = String(payload['type'] ?? '')
   102→
   103→    if (payloadType === 'message') {
   104→      const role = String(payload['role'] ?? '').toLowerCase()
   105→      if (role === 'user' || role === 'assistant') {
   106→        const text = extractTextBlocks(payload['content'])
   107→        if (text) {
   108→          messages.push({ role, text, timestamp })
   109→        }
   110→      }
   111→      continue
   112→    }
   113→
   114→    if (payloadType === 'user_message' || payloadType === 'agent_message') {
   115→      const role = payloadType === 'user_message' ? 'user' : 'assistant'
   116→      const text = String(payload['message'] ?? '').trim()
   117→      if (text) {
   118→        messages.push({ role, text, timestamp })
   119→      }
   120→      continue
   121→    }
   122→
   123→    if (payloadType === 'function_call') {
   124→      const name = String(payload['name'] ?? '') || 'function_call'
   125→      const args = payload['arguments'] ?? payload['input']
   126→      toolEvents.push({
   127→        summary: `${name} input=${summarizeValue(args)}`,
   128→        timestamp,
   129→      })
   130→      continue
   131→    }
   132→
   133→    if (payloadType === 'custom_tool_call') {
   134→      const name = String(payload['name'] ?? '') || String(payload['call_id'] ?? '') || 'custom_tool_call'
   135→      toolEvents.push({
   136→        summary: `${name} input=${summarizeValue(payload['input'])}`,
   137→        timestamp,
   138→      })
   139→      continue
   140→    }
   141→
   142→    if (payloadType === 'function_call_output') {
   143→      const name = String(payload['name'] ?? '') || String(payload['call_id'] ?? '') || 'function_call_output'
   144→      const output = payload['output'] ?? payload['content']
   145→      toolEvents.push({
   146→        summary: `${name} output=${summarizeValue(output)}`,
   147→        timestamp,
   148→      })
   149→      continue
   150→    }
   151→
   152→    if (payloadType === 'custom_tool_call_output') {
   153→      const name = String(payload['name'] ?? '') || String(payload['call_id'] ?? '') || 'custom_tool_call_output'
   154→      const output = payload['output'] ?? payload['content']
   155→      toolEvents.push({
   156→        summary: `${name} output=${summarizeValue(output)}`,
   157→        timestamp,
   158→      })
   159→    }
   160→  }
   161→
   162→  return {
   163→    client: 'codex',
   164→    session_id: sessionId,
   165→    title,
   166→    started_at: startedAt,
   167→    cwd,
   168→    branch,
   169→    messages: deduplicateMessages(messages),
   170→    tool_events: deduplicateToolEvents(toolEvents),
   171→    source_path: filePath,
   172→  }
   173→}

In the majority of turns the timestamps match and dedup works. But in approximately 18 % of turns (confirmed in a 94-message production session: 14 out of 76 assistant turns) the two representations carry timestamps that differ by exactly 1 ms. Different timestamps → different dedup keys → **the same message appears twice** in the clean transcript.\n\n### Evidence (session 019cf4b1, openmnemo project)\n\n```\npayload.type=agent_message   ts=2026-03-16T03:32:48.264Z  text=\"这个仓库原 README 写的...\"\npayload.type=message(asst)   ts=2026-03-16T03:32:48.265Z  text=\"这个仓库原 README 写的...\"\n→ different dedup keys → duplicated in clean output\n```\n\n14 out of 76 assistant messages are affected in this session alone.\n\n---\n\n## Bug 2 — System context injection appears as first user message\n\n### Root cause\n\nThe Codex CLI injects system context as the very first `message(role=user)` record of every session. This single record contains:\n\n- `# AGENTS.md instructions for <path>` — full project AGENTS.md\n- `<INSTRUCTIONS>` — all installed skill definitions\n- `<environment_context>` — cwd, date, timezone, shell\n- `<permissions instructions>` — filesystem sandbox policy\n- `<collaboration_mode>` — agent collaboration mode\n\nThe parser includes this verbatim as **Message #1** in the clean transcript. In a typical session, this injection is 200–400 lines long. The actual user question does not appear until Message #2, making the clean transcript look like it contains no real conversation.\n\n### Impact\n\n- Users reading the clean transcript cannot find their own messages\n- Search and vector indexing over clean transcripts is dominated by repeated system boilerplate\n- The clean transcript defeats its own purpose as a readable session record\n\n---\n\n## Affected versions\n\nConfirmed on Codex CLI `0.114.0`, JSONL format with `session_meta` + `response_item` + `event_msg` records.\n\n---\n\n## Proposed fix\n\nSee PR #6 (linked below).\n\n**Bug 1**: Collect `response_item / payload.type=message` records as the canonical source. Collect `event_msg / payload.type=agent_message|user_message` records separately as a fallback, used only when no canonical records exist (backward-compatible with older Codex versions that emit only streaming events). Never mix the two sets.\n\n**Bug 2**: Add `isCodexSystemInjection(text)` that detects the known injection markers and silently filters matching messages from both the canonical and streaming paths.\n\nBoth fixes come with regression tests. All 401 existing tests continue to pass.\nEOF\n)\"",

2. Key Technical Concepts:
- MemoryTree (memorytree-workflow skill): A cross-client AI conversation memory system supporting Codex, Claude Code, and Gemini CLI
- Transcript pipeline: raw JSONL → clean Markdown + manifest JSON, stored in Memory/06_transcripts/{raw,clean,manifests}/
- Codex JSONL double-encoding: Every message turn appears twice — as event_msg (streaming, payload.type=agent_message/user_message) AND as response_item (canonical, payload.type=message)
- Timestamp jitter bug: The two encodings differ by ~1ms in ~18% of turns, defeating timestamp+role+contentHash deduplication in deduplicateMessages()
- System context injection: Codex CLI injects AGENTS.md, skill definitions, environment metadata, and permissions as the first message(role=user) record in every session
- deterministic-code cleaning mode: The clean transcript is generated by writeCleanMarkdown() from parsed messages[] and tool_events[]
- Two-list strategy: Separating canonical messages from streamingMessages (fallback) in parseCodexTranscript
- isCodexSystemInjection(text): New exported function to detect and filter system injection markers
- Global vs repo-local archive: ~/.memorytree/ is the global archive; Memory/06_transcripts/ is the repo-local mirror (only current project's transcripts)
- Heartbeat daemon: Background process that auto-imports transcripts every 5 minutes with auto_push=true configured for openmnemo only

     export function parseCodexTranscript(filePath: string): ParsedTranscript {
       // ...
       // Canonical messages from `payload.type === 'message'` (response_item records).
       const messages: TranscriptMessage[] = []
       // Streaming fallback: `agent_message` / `user_message` from event_msg records.
       // The Codex CLI double-encodes every message: each turn fires as a streaming
       // `event_msg` (agent_message / user_message) AND later as a canonical
       // `response_item` (message). Processing both causes duplicates because the two
       // representations share almost-identical but not always equal timestamps
       // (millisecond jitter), defeating timestamp-based deduplication. We therefore
       // prefer canonical records and use streaming records only as a fallback for
       // sessions recorded by older Codex versions that emit only streaming events.
       const streamingMessages: TranscriptMessage[] = []
       
       // In message handler:
       if (payloadType === 'message') {
         const role = String(payload['role'] ?? '').toLowerCase()
         if (role === 'user' || role === 'assistant') {
           const text = extractTextBlocks(payload['content'])
           if (text && !isCodexSystemInjection(text)) {
             messages.push({ role, text, timestamp })
           }
         }
         continue
       }
       
       // Streaming events collected separately, never mixed with canonical:
       if (payloadType === 'user_message' || payloadType === 'agent_message') {
         const role = payloadType === 'user_message' ? 'user' : 'assistant'
         const text = String(payload['message'] ?? '').trim()
         if (text && !isCodexSystemInjection(text)) {
           streamingMessages.push({ role, text, timestamp })
         }
         continue
       }
       
       // Use canonical records when available; fall back to streaming events otherwise.
       const finalMessages = messages.length > 0 ? messages : streamingMessages
       // ...
     }

     // Injection markers:
     const CODEX_INJECTION_MARKERS: readonly string[] = [
       '<INSTRUCTIONS>',
       '<environment_context>',
       '<permissions instructions>',
       '<collaboration_mode>',
       '# AGENTS.md instructions for',
     ]

     export function isCodexSystemInjection(text: string): boolean {
       return CODEX_INJECTION_MARKERS.some(marker => text.includes(marker))
     }

Fixes #13

## What this changes

Two bugs in `parseCodexTranscript` (`src/transcript/parse.ts`) corrupted clean transcripts for every real-world Codex session.

### Bug 1 — duplicate messages from double-encoded JSONL records

The Codex CLI writes every message turn twice: once as a streaming `event_msg` (`payload.type=agent_message` / `user_message`) and again as a canonical `response_item` (`payload.type=message`). The parser handled both, then relied on `deduplicateMessages` to eliminate duplicates using a key of `timestamp + role + contentHash`. The two representations carry timestamps that differ by up to ~1 ms, producing different dedup keys and causing ~18 % of turns to appear twice.

**Fix**: collect canonical `message` records exclusively into the `messages` list. Collect streaming events into a separate `streamingMessages` list that is used only when no canonical records were found — preserving backward compatibility with older Codex versions that emit only `event_msg` records.

### Bug 2 — system context injection included as user messages

The Codex CLI injects AGENTS.md instructions, skill definitions, environment metadata, permissions, and collaboration-mode config as the first `message(role=user)` record of every session. This appeared verbatim as Message #1 in the clean transcript, hiding the real conversation behind 200–400 lines of system boilerplate.

**Fix**: add `isCodexSystemInjection(text)` (exported for testing) that checks for the known injection markers:

```
<INSTRUCTIONS>
<environment_context>
<permissions instructions>
<collaboration_mode>
# AGENTS.md instructions for
```
assistant #191 08:28:22

PR #14 is open and ready. Issue #13 is linked. The fix is complete with 401/401 tests passing.

Summary of what was accomplished:

- Issue #13: Filed at https://github.com/beyondchenlin/memorytree-workflow/issues/13 documenting two bugs in parseCodexTranscript
- PR #14: Filed at https://github.com/beyondchenlin/memorytree-workflow/pull/14 with a complete fix:
- Bug 1 (duplicates): Two-list strategy — canonical message records go to messages[], streaming agent_message/user_message go to streamingMessages[] (fallback only). Eliminates the ~18% duplicate rate from 1ms timestamp jitter between the two encodings.
- Bug 2 (injection): New isCodexSystemInjection() filters the first system-context user message (AGENTS.md, skill definitions, environment metadata) that was appearing verbatim as Message #1 in every clean transcript.
- 14 new tests covering both code paths, plus isCodexSystemInjection unit tests
- 401/401 tests pass, typecheck clean, build successful

   156→      )

   158→  } else {
   159→    lines.push(
   160→      'No user or assistant messages were extracted deterministically from the source transcript.',
   161→      '',
   162→    )
   163→  }
   164→
   165→  lines.push('## Tool Events')
   166→  if (parsed.tool_events.length > 0) {
   167→    for (const event of parsed.tool_events) {
   168→      lines.push(`- \`${event.timestamp ?? manifest.started_at}\` ${event.summary}`)
   169→    }
   170→  } else {
   171→    lines.push('- No tool events were extracted.')
   172→  }
   173→  lines.push('')
   174→
   175→  writeFileSync(filePath, lines.join('\n'), 'utf-8')
   176→}
   177→
   178→export function preserveExistingImportTimestamp(
   179→  existing: Record<string, unknown> | null,
   180→  payload: ManifestEntry,
   181→): ManifestEntry {
   182→  if (existing === null) return payload
   183→  const payloadRecord = { ...payload } as Record<string, unknown>

## Summary

Two bugs in `parseCodexTranscript` corrupt the clean transcript for every real-world Codex session.

---

## Bug 1 — Duplicate assistant messages (~18 % of turns)

### Root cause

===
title:	fix(codex-parser): eliminate duplicate messages and filter system injections
state:	OPEN
author:	beyondchenlin
labels:	
assignees:	
reviewers:	
projects:	
milestone:	
number:	14
url:	https://github.com/beyondchenlin/memorytree-workflow/pull/14
additions:	215
deletions:	21
auto-merge:	disabled
--
Fixes #13

## What this changes

Two bugs in `parseCodexTranscript` (`src/transcript/parse.ts`) corrupted clean transcripts for every real-world Codex session.

### Bug 1 — duplicate messages from double-encoded JSONL records

The Codex CLI writes every message turn twice: once as a streaming `event_msg` (`payload.type=agent_message` / `user_message`) and again as a canonical `response_item` (`payload.type=message`). The parser handled both, then relied on `deduplicateMessages` to eliminate duplicates using a key of `timestamp + role + contentHash`. The two representations carry timestamps that differ by up to ~1 ms, producing different dedup keys and causing ~18 % of turns to appear twice.

**Fix**: collect canonical `message` records exclusively into the `messages` list. Collect streaming events into a separate `streamingMessages` list that is used only when no canonical records were found — preserving backward compatibility with older Codex versions that emit only `event_msg` records.
