Expand full message

这个方向很好，我来系统梳理一下思路。

---

## 开源 Markdown → 网站项目评估

| 项目 | 语言 | 适合度 | 备注 |
|------|------|--------|------|
| Quartz | TypeScript | ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐ | 专为 Obsidian 式知识库设计，双向链接，内置全文搜索，和 Memory/ 结构天然契合 |
| MkDocs Material | Python | ⭐⭐⭐⭐ | 文档类最漂亮，已有 Python 环境，支持 Chart.js 插件 |
| VitePress | Node.js | ⭐⭐⭐ | 现代快，但偏文档向，定制 dashboard 需要写 Vue 组件 |
| 自建生成器 | Node.js | ⭐⭐⭐⭐ | 最灵活，零外部依赖，嵌入心跳流畅，但初期工作量大 |

我的建议：自建 Node.js 生成器 + Chart.js

原因：
- memorytree-workflow 本身已是 Node.js，新增 memorytree report 命令无缝集成
- 生成 自包含 HTML（CSS/JS inline），不依赖服务器，直接双击打开或部署
- 心跳里直接 node dist/cli.js report build --root ... 触发
- PDF 用 Puppeteer（已是 Node.js 生态）一行导出

---

## 网站架构设计

Memory/07_reports/
├── index.html              ← 总 Dashboard
├── transcripts/
│   ├── index.html          ← 所有会话列表
│   ├── codex/
│   │   └── {session}.html  ← 单次 Codex 会话页
│   └── claude/
│       └── {session}.html  ← 单次 Claude 会话页
├── goals/
│   └── index.html          ← 目标历史时间线
├── knowledge/
│   └── index.html          ← 知识库文章列表
└── export/
    └── {date}-report.pdf   ← 心跳定期导出 PDF

---

### 1. index.html — 总 Dashboard
全部代码计算，零 AI token

├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤

└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

---

## 代码计算 vs AI 摘要 分工

| 部分 | 方式 | 原因 |
|------|------|------|
| 消息数、工具调用数、时长 | 代码 | 确定性，零成本 |
| Activity Heatmap | 代码 | 按时间戳聚合 |
| Client 分布、Top Tools | 代码 | 简单计数 |
| 会话摘要（2-3句话） | LLM | 只有这里值得花 token |
| 摘要缓存 | .cache/{sha256}.json | 同一 raw SHA 不重复请求 |

---

## 心跳集成方式

heartbeat run-once
  → discover transcripts
  → import new ones
  → report build --root . --skip-ai-if-cached   ← 新增这步
  → git commit memorytree/openmnemo
  → push

AI 摘要只在首次导入时调用一次，之后缓存命中直接跳过。

---

HEARTBEAT FLOW (src/heartbeat/heartbeat.ts)\n\n**Entry Point: `main()`**\n\n1. **Lock Acquisition** – Prevents concurrent heartbeat runs\n   - Uses PID-based lock file at `~/.memorytree/heartbeat.lock`\n   - Checks if stored PID is alive; reclaims stale locks\n   - Returns 0 if already running (not an error)\n\n2. **Load Configuration** – From `~/.memorytree/config.toml`\n   - `heartbeat_interval` (e.g., \"5m\", default)\n   - `projects` – Array of `{path, name}`\n   - `auto_push` – Whether to push transcripts to Git\n   - `log_level` – debug\\|info\\|warn\\|error\n\n3. **Per-Project Processing** – `processProject()`\n   - Discover source files from `~/.codex`, `~/.claude`, `~/.gemini`\n   - Parse each source into `ParsedTranscript`\n   - Skip if no content (no messages/tool_events)\n   - **Key: Check if transcript matches repo** – via `transcriptMatchesRepo()`\n     - Compares `cwd` in transcript with repo root\n     - Falls back to slug matching if cwd doesn't match\n   - **Sensitive pattern scanning** – Regex patterns for API keys, passwords, tokens\n   - **Import transcript** – Calls `importTranscript()` with:\n     - `parsed` transcript\n     - `projectPath` (repo root)\n     - `globalRoot` (default: `~/.memorytree/transcripts`)\n     - `projectSlug` (derived from project name)\n     - `rawUploadPermission` (not-set\\|approved\\|denied)\n     - `mirrorToRepo=true` – Also store in `Memory/06_transcripts/`\n\n4. **Git Operations** – After import\n   - Check for changes in `Memory/` directory\n   - Commit with message: `memorytree(transcripts): import N transcript(s)`\n   - If `auto_push` enabled: push to remote (with retry)\n   - Write alerts on failure (threshold-based)\n\n5. **Lock Release** – Always called in finally block\n\n### 5. IMPORT ORCHESTRATION (src/transcript/import.ts)\n\n**Function: `importTranscript(parsed, root, globalRoot, projectSlug, rawUploadPermission, mirrorToRepo)`**\n\n**File Paths:**\n```\n# Session label from session_id or filename stem\nsessionLabel = slugify(session_id)\nartifactStem = \"${sessionLabel}__${rawSha256.slice(0, 8)}\"\n\n# Year/Month partition from started_at timestamp\n[yearToken, monthToken] = timestampPartition(started_at)\nsourceSuffix = file extension of original\n\n# Repo mirror (if mirrorToRepo=true)\nMemory/06_transcripts/\n├── raw/{client}/{year}/{month}/{artifactStem}{sourceSuffix}\n├── clean/{client}/{year}/{month}/{artifactStem}.md\n└── manifests/{client}/{year}/{month}/{artifactStem}.json\n\n# Global storage\n~/.memorytree/transcripts/\n├── raw/{client}/{project}/{year}/{month}/{artifactStem}{sourceSuffix}\n├── clean/{client}/{project}/{year}/{month}/{artifactStem}.md\n├── index/\n│   ├── manifests/{client}/{project}/{year}/{month}/{artifactStem}.json\n│   ├── sessions.jsonl  (append-only log of manifest entries)\n│   └── search.sqlite   (sql.js upsert)\n```\n\n**Processing Steps:**\n\n1. **Compute paths** – Create directories recursively\n2. **Copy raw source** – To both repo and global locations\n3. **Build manifest** – `ManifestEntry` object with all metadata\n4. **Preserve import timestamp** – If existing manifest has same content signature, keep old `imported_at`\n5. **Write clean markdown** – YAML frontmatter + messages + metadata\n6. **Write manifest JSON** – To both repo and global locations\n7. **Append event log** – Only if manifest changed (content-wise)\n8. **Upsert search index** – SQLite table via `sql.js`\n\n**Return: `ManifestEntry`** – Can be printed as JSON or formatted text\n\n### 6. TRANSCRIPT PARSING (src/transcript/parse.ts)\n\n**Client Inference: `inferClient(client, sourcePath)`**\n\nAuto-detection based on path patterns:\n- `/.codex/` or filename `rollout-*` → `codex`\n- `/.claude/` or `/projects/` → `claude`\n- `/.gemini/` or `checkpoint` → `gemini`\n\n**Three Client-Specific Parsers:**\n\n**Codex Parser (`parseCodexTranscript`)**\n- Format: JSONL records with `type` field\n- Types: `session_meta`, `response_item`, `event_msg`\n- Messages: From `type=message` records (canonical), fallback to `type=user_message`/`agent_message`\n- Tool events: `function_call`, `custom_tool_call`, `*_output`\n- **Deduplication:** Uses streaming events only if no canonical records (avoids double-recording)\n- **System injection filter:** Skips first message if contains `<INSTRUCTIONS>`, `<environment_context>`, etc.\n\n**Claude Parser (`parseClaudeTranscript`)**\n- Format: JSONL with `type` field (`user` or `assistant`)\n- Message content: String or block array with `{type, text}` objects\n- Block types: `input_text`, `output_text`, `text` (text), `tool_use`, `tool_result` (tools)\n- Skip blocks: `thinking`, `reasoning`\n- Metadata: `sessionId`, `cwd`, `gitBranch` from any record\n\n**Gemini Parser (`parseGeminiTranscript`)**\n- Format: JSONL or JSON\n- Recursive tree traversal to find:\n  - Metadata: `sessionId`, `chatId`, `cwd`, `branch`, `timestamp`\n  - Messages: `role` in (user, model, assistant); extract text from `parts`, `content`, `text`, `message`\n  - Tool events: `toolName`, `functionName`, `tool`\n- Flexible structure to handle nested conversations\n\n**Common Utilities (src/transcript/common.ts):**\n\n- **Slugify**: Removes non-ASCII, converts to lowercase, replaces spaces/special chars with hyphens\n- **SHA256**: File hash (raw), content hash (16-char prefix for dedup)\n- **Timestamp normalization**: Unix seconds → ISO 8601, handle timezone offsets\n- **Timestamp partition**: Extract year/month for directory structure\n- **Deduplication**: Track signature (`timestamp\\0role\\0contentHash`) to skip duplicates\n- **Text extraction**: From nested blocks, handles Gemini multi-part messages\n- **YAML escaping**: For frontmatter values\n\n### 7. DISCOVERY (src/transcript/discover.ts)\n\n**File Patterns per Client:**\n\n```typescript\nconst CLIENT_PATTERNS = {\n  codex: ['sessions/**/*.jsonl'],\n  claude: ['projects/**/*.jsonl'],\n  gemini: [\n    'tmp/*/checkpoints/**/*.json',\n    'tmp/*/checkpoints/**/*.jsonl',\n    'history/**/*.json',\n    'history/**/*.jsonl',\n    'chats/**/*.json',\n    'chats/**/*.jsonl',\n  ],\n}\n```\n\n**Function: `discoverSourceFiles(clients?, roots?)`**\n\n- Scans default roots: `~/.codex`, `~/.claude`, `~/.gemini`\n- Uses `fast-glob` for pattern matching\n- **Sorting**: By modification time (newest first), then by path (reverse alphabetical)\n- **Deduplication**: Tracks lowercase paths to avoid duplicates\n- Returns: `Array<[client, filePath]>`\n\n**Project Slug Inference: `inferProjectSlug(parsed)`**\n\n1. Fallback: `unknown-project`\n\n**Repo Matching: `transcriptMatchesRepo(parsed, repoRoot, repoSlug)`**\n\n- Exact match: `parsed.cwd === repoRoot`\n- Parent match: `cwd` is under `repoRoot`\n- Slug match: Project slugs match and not `unknown-project`\n\n### 8. SEARCH INDEX (src/transcript/db.ts)\n\n**Technology: `sql.js` (WebAssembly SQLite)**\n\nAllows in-memory or persistent SQLite without native bindings.\n\n**Schema:**\n\n```sql\nCREATE TABLE transcripts (\n  client TEXT NOT NULL,\n  project TEXT NOT NULL,\n  session_id TEXT NOT NULL,\n  raw_sha256 TEXT NOT NULL,\n  title TEXT,\n  started_at TEXT,\n  imported_at TEXT,\n  cwd TEXT,\n  branch TEXT,\n  raw_source_path TEXT,\n  raw_upload_permission TEXT,\n  global_raw_path TEXT,\n  global_clean_path TEXT,\n  repo_raw_path TEXT,\n  repo_clean_path TEXT,\n  repo_manifest_path TEXT,\n  message_count INTEGER,\n  tool_event_count INTEGER,\n  PRIMARY KEY (client, project, session_id, raw_sha256)\n)\n```\n\n**Function: `upsertSearchIndex(dbPath, manifest)`**\n\n- Loads existing database or creates new one\n- Executes upsert: Insert on conflict updates data columns\n- Exports WASM database to binary file\n- Lazy initialization: `sql.js` WASM loaded once per process\n\n### 9. deduplicates\n- `extractToolNames`: returns top-N by count, ties sorted alphabetically for determinism\n- Client counts: codex/claude/gemini split\n\n**`tests/report/render/charts.test.ts`**\n- `renderHeatmap` with empty input renders 365 cells all level-0\n- `renderHeatmap` with a day at count 7 emits level-3 color\n- `renderClientDoughnut` with all-zero counts does not divide by zero bracket]`\n\n**`tests/report/render/search.test.ts`**\n- `buildSearchIndex` truncates text at 50 kB\n- `renderSearchPage` embeds index as valid JSON (test with `JSON.parse`)\n- URL format is correctly\n- `buildSummaryPrompt` truncates at 30 messages, truncates each message text at 500 chars\n- `getSummary` returns `''` when `noAi: true` without calling the SDK\n- `getSummary` returns `''` when `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` is absent (mock `process.env`)\n- `getSummary` returns cached value without calling the SDK when cache hit\n\n**`tests/heartbeat/config.test.ts` additions**\n- `loadConfig` reads `generate_report = true` correctly\n- `loadConfig` defaults `generate_report` to `false` when absent\n- `loadConfig` reads `ai_summary_model` string\n- `saveConfig` round-trips both new fields\n\n### Integration tests\n\n**`tests/report/build.test.ts`**\n- Scaffold a minimal `Memory/06_transcripts/manifests/` tree with 2 manifest JSON files and matching clean markdown files in a `mkdtempSync` temp dir\n- Call `buildReport({ root, output, noAi: true, pdf: false })`\n- Assert that `index.html`, `transcripts/index.html`, `search.html`, `knowledge/index.html`, `goals/index.html` exist\n- `cmdReportBuild` returns exit code 0 for a valid but empty Memory tree\n\n### What NOT to unit test\n- The full SVG path math (it is visual, verified by inspection)\n- The Anthropic API call itself (mock only; never call real API in tests)\n- CSS string content\n\n---\n\n## 9. Gotchas and Edge Cases\n\n### Manifest loading\n`Memory/06_transcripts/manifests/` is partitioned by `client/year/month/`. Use `fast-glob` pattern `Memory/06_transcripts/manifests/**/*.json` — the same glob package is already a dependency. Sort by `started_at` for stable output ordering.\n\n### Clean markdown path resolution\n`manifest.repo_clean_path` is a POSIX-relative path (e.g. `Memory/06_transcripts/clean/...`). Use `join(root, manifest.repo_clean_path)` to resolve it. Some manifests may have `repo_mirror_enabled: false` and an empty `repo_clean_path` — in that case fall back to `manifest.global_clean_path`. Always guard with `existsSync` and return `''` on missing files.\n\n### `--no-ai` Commander.js flag gotcha\nCommander treats `--no-<name>` as a boolean negation flag. The option declared as `.option('--no-ai', ...)` will populate `opts.ai` as `false` when passed and `true` by default. The `noAi` property must be `!opts.ai`. This matches the existing `--no-<x>` patterns in Commander.\n\n### `@anthropic-ai/sdk` optional dependency\nThe SDK import must be dynamic (`await import('@anthropic-ai/sdk')`), placed inside a try/catch that returns `''` on `MODULE_NOT_FOUND`. This way the package is truly optional — the build still works even if the user hasn't installed it. Add to `package.json` as a regular dependency (not optional), but the code must defensively handle its absence for the period before npm install is re-run.\n\n### HTML escaping\nAll user-generated content (titles, session IDs, message text, file paths) that is interpolated into HTML strings must be HTML-escaped. Write a small `escHtml(s: string): string` utility in `render/layout.ts` that handles `& < > \" '`. This is the most common XSS source in template-style HTML generation.\n\n### File system on Windows\nThe project runs on Windows (confirmed by the platform info). All path construction must use `node:path` `join()`, not string concatenation with `/`. The `toPosixPath` utility from `src/utils/path.ts` is already available for converting before writing into HTML href attributes.\n\n### Large transcript sets\n`buildReport` must not hold all parsed transcript content in memory simultaneously. Process transcripts in a streaming fashion: parse → summarize → render → write → discard. Keep only manifests (small) in memory throughout. The summary concurrency limit (5 parallel) also limits peak memory.\n\n### `.gitignore` for `Memory/07_reports/`\nThe requirements specify the output dir should not be committed. The `cmd-report.ts` or `build.ts` should check if `Memory/07_reports` is already in `.gitignore` and append it if not. Alternatively document this as a manual step, since the `init` command scaffolds `.gitignore` already — the safer approach is to add `Memory/07_reports/` to the default gitignore template in `src/project/scaffold.ts`.\n\n### Wiki-link regex\nThe `[[session-id]]` pattern must use a non-greedy match: `/\\[\\[([^\\]]+?)\\]\\]/g`. Session stems can contain hyphens and underscores but not `]]`. The regex must not match across newlines.\n\n### Empty / single-data-point charts\n- Doughnut with all zeros: render an empty gray ring, no percentage labels.\n- Line chart with 1 data point: render a single dot (circle), not a path.\n- Heatmap with no data: render all gray cells (still useful as a date grid).\n- Bar chart with no tools: render the SVG with a \"No tool events recorded\" text node.\n\n### `serve` command port conflicts\nWrap the HTTP server creation in a try/catch for `EADDRINUSE`. Print a clear message: `\"Port NNNN is in use. Try --port MMMM.\"` and exit with code 1.\n\n### Report cache invalidation\nThe cache key is `raw_sha256` (the SHA256 of the raw source file). This means the cache entry is permanently valid as long as the source file has not changed — which is the correct invariant. No TTL is needed.\n\n---\n\n## 10. Implementation Sequence\n\n1. **`src/types/report.ts`** — all types first\n2. **`src/report/render/css.ts`** — CSS constant (pure string, no deps)\n3. **`src/report/render/layout.ts`** — `htmlShell`, `renderNav`, `escHtml`\n4. **`src/report/stats.ts`** — `computeStats` and sub-helpers (pure, fully testable without I/O)\n5. **`src/report/render/charts.ts`** — SVG functions (pure)\n6. **`src/report/render/links.ts`** — `buildLinkGraph` (pure, takes content as string)\n7. **`src/report/render/search.ts`** — `buildSearchIndex`, `renderSearchPage`\n8. **`src/report/render/dashboard.ts`**, `transcript-list.ts`, `transcript.ts`, `knowledge.ts`, `goals.ts`\n9. **`src/report/summarize.ts`** — AI integration (isolated, mockable)\n10. **`src/report/build.ts`** — orchestrator tying everything together\n11. **`src/cli/cmd-report.ts`** — thin CLI adapter\n12. **Modify `src/cli/main.ts`** — register `report` command\n13. **Modify `src/heartbeat/config.ts`** — add two new fields\n14. **Modify `src/heartbeat/heartbeat.ts`** — call `buildReport` if configured\n15. **Modify `package.json`** — add `@anthropic-ai/sdk`\n16. **`tests/report/stats.test.ts`**, `charts.test.ts`, `links.test.ts`, `search.test.ts`, `summarize.test.ts`\n17. **`tests/report/build.test.ts`** — integration test with temp dir\n\n---\n\n### Critical Files for Implementation\n\n- `C:/Users/ai/.codex/skills/memorytree-workflow/src/cli/main.ts` -
